# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Mistral Large 2

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.0)
    The story attempts thematic depth with its exploration of self-deception and reality versus dreams, but relies too heavily on explicit statements rather than allowing meaning to emerge through action. The ending provides resolution but feels somewhat predictable. While there are effective symbolic elements (moon phases, statues), the story lacks the emotional resonance or surprising insight that would elevate it to exceptional storytelling.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=4.5)
    The story attempts thematic depth with its exploration of healing and reimagined endings, but relies too heavily on telling rather than showing these concepts. The emotional transformation of both Edmund and the widow feels unearned due to insufficient development. The bee pin's symbolic potential remains largely unexplored, and the story's resolution feels rushed rather than resonant.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=4.3)
    The story attempts thematic depth with its exploration of potential and self-discovery, but relies on abstract statements rather than concrete scenes to convey meaning. The prose tends toward telling rather than showing, particularly in describing Silas's transformation. The central conflict lacks sufficient complexity, and the resolution feels unearned without showing the specific challenges Silas overcomes.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=4.5)
    The story relies heavily on telling rather than showing, particularly regarding emotional states and character development. Metaphors like "heart a maggoty wooden chest" feel disconnected from the narrative. The theme of forgiveness is explicitly stated rather than emerging naturally, and the resolution lacks the complexity needed for genuine emotional impact.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=4.3)

The AI metaphor feels underdeveloped, and the resolution lacks emotional impact. The writing relies heavily on exposition rather than scene-building, with minimal dialogue or character interaction. The ending feels rushed and overly neat, missing opportunities for deeper reflection or ambiguity.
